[28/02/24, 12:00:47‚ÄØPM] ~‚ÄØLion Dr S Raghavendra Babu: The Chief Commissioner
Bruhat Bengaluru  Mahanagara Palike 
N R Square
Bangalore - 560002

Dear Sir,

                     Sub : Objection on BBMP's Proposal to Calculate Property Tax based on Guidance Value                                                   

I as an individual home owner raise objection to the BBMP's proposal of calculating Property Tax based on Guidance Value , for the following reasons :

1. Guidance Value of the property has no relevance to the Property Tax . It is  absolutely illogical as Guidance Value differs from area to area in the City whereas the services like roads construction / maintenance , water supply ,  sewage collection / disposal and other services are provided equitably to all areas irrespective of the  different Guidance Value. It would therefore be totally irrational to calculate Property Tax based on Guidance Value. 

2. Sir , it is a known fact that a significant number of Property owners do noy pay property tax in Bengaluru. It is therefore sad that  Instead of collecting Property Taxes due to BBMP from such defaulters , the Owners who are regularly paying Property Tax are being imposed a Guidance Value based tax which is not tenable. 

3. Citizens have NO control over the Guidance value fixed/revised by the Government almost every year predominantly meant to garner registration stamp duty charges .

4. Guidance Value is for  buying and selling  of a property , as and when it is transacted . It therefore should not be linked to the Property tax which is paid every year. Market / Guidance value comes into picture only when one is selling the property for which Govt is paid the stamp duty for the transaction.

5. For a person/family living in a house/flat/apartment and having a roof over the head, Guidance Value has absolutely no meaning until one decides to sell.

6. In addition to the increase in tax due to revision in guidance value you are also proposing 5% increase in the property tax every year which is a double whammy.

7. You have given 20% increase every year until it matches the full tax value but this is only a temporary relief with sword dangling as the years pass by.

8. On the whole this is a huge burden as an individual home owner already reeling under high cost of living in Bangalore. Present way of calculating Property Tax is rational. BBMP can review and revise it from time to time by a reasonable percentage. 

Keeping in view of the above , I appeal to your good office to drop the proposal of calculating Property Tax based on  the Guidance Value which is absolutely not  rationale , logical and fair to the citizens of Bengaluru.
